shortcoming:
1. I arrived at the hotel early in the morning and entered the parking lot. There was no one to guide me, so I walked around the parking lot by myself for more than 10 minutes.
2. No one opened the door or helped with the luggage.
3. The hotel lobby was extremely lively in the early morning. I thought I was at the Workers' Stadium.
4. The hotel facilities are older, the lights are dim, the sofas are stained, the chairs are movable, and the water in the bathtub needs to be filled for 3 or 4 minutes before it is barely warm.
5. Because I was sick, I asked the front desk if takeout could be delivered to the room. The answer was that there is no such service. If you have a fever at night, you have to go downstairs to get medicine.
6. Smoking is blatant in the elevator. I can pretend I didn‚Äôt see you smoking in the lobby. Smoking in a confined space in the elevator is damning.
7. The parking spaces provided by the hotel are not free, but 50% off! From the beginning, the staff told me that you scan me, and just drive out after scanning. When I arrived at the door, I was told that it was 10 yuan for an hour. If you parked for 10 hours, the discount for 100 yuan was 52. If you wanted to charge, you could just charge me. He told me to give me a coupon and let me drive away, but no one stopped me at the door.
